                      <div data-reactid="455">
                       This one bedroom 1 bath bungalow is walking distance to great hiking (Temescal Canyon) and the beach as well as the village of Pacific Palisades. Fully furnished with all the amenities for comfort including beach toys (boogie boards, beach chairs).
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="456">
                       Architectural charm and the ability to WALK not drive everywhere are just a couple of the features of this 1920's bungalow. It comfortably sleeps 4, (one queen bed, two twin sleeper sofas), includes all bed linens and towels, a washer/dryer/dishwasher, ceiling fan and AC unit. 
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="457">
                       The enclave of the Pacific Palisades has a Norman Rockwell charm, family friendly with chic shops like Elyssse Walker, great restaurants like Maison Gerard, and fantastic farmers market, bike friendly, yogurt shops, antique stores, destination worthy hiking, etc. etc. Its only a mile from Santa Monica's Pier and trendy bars, and 3 miles from all that Venice has to offer. In the other direction is the surf capitol Malibu (only a 10 minute drive to 1st Point). See more at: (URL HIDDEN)

                      <div data-reactid="1155">
                       You will love this cozy room! This room can accommodate up to two people comfortably with the queen sized bed and your very own private bathroom + shower and parking spot. This is a great alternative to any hotel room and very affordable. Update 24/2/17: Check out the guidebook with some of our favorite spots around LA! There is also an extra inflatable mattress available and a new shower head! There are great restaurants, bars and coffee shops within easy walking distance. We will inform you on our favorites when you arrive! We're only 3 miles from the beach so you can get a change of scenery quite quickly and easily. This neighborhood is extremely safe and friendly. There are many UCLA students in the area as well as young professionals. WE ARE: 2.3 miles from The Getty Museum 2.6 miles from UCLA 5.0 miles from Venice Beach 7.6 miles from West Hollywood 15 miles to Downtown Los Angeles 20 miles from Malibu Guests have access to the kitchen and living room. Ralph's supermarket is walking distance of the apartment and there is lots of fridge space available for you and a guest! You are welcome to enjoy Netflix and PS4 on the large flat screen and also the free WiFi. We're both outgoing and love to make new friends. We are very happy to give insight on awesome local restaurants, coffee shops and activities, etc. But, if you don't have time or interest in socializing, we are happy to accommodate! We are home often - studying and working but also like to enjoy the Los Angeles sun down at Santa Monica beach front (only 3 miles away). Come along with us! Our neighborhood is safe, friendly. We love how close we are to everything - coffee, food and fun! We're near a few bus stops - you can get just about anywhere from our place. If you don't feel like taking the bus - most of our guests use the Uber or Lyft service to get around which is a safe, friendly and decently priced alternative to the bus. If you have your own vehicle or happen to rent a vehicle, you will receive your very own private parking spot. (Not easy to come by in Los Angeles). 3 people max. Reminder: There is only one queen-sized bed in this room + inflatable mattress if needed.
